36:1565:97335:0:8:245:249:456:10:g_d0_f20:10:g_d0_f20:[
36:1566:97336:8:0:249:302:448:10:g_d0_f16:10:g_d0_f9:A(1−τdisc)
36:1567:97346:0:22:302:310:456:10:g_d0_f20:7:g_d0_f12:]2
36:1568:97348:22:0:275:280:434:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:2
36:1569:97349:0:31:314:540:441:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:+νmm−1 ̃πdisc+νIR(Rz2−Γ),(71)
36:1570:97378:31:16:86:540:410:10:g_d0_f16:10:g_d0_f9:Wdisc(A,i,m−1) is the welfare of the old agents when the tax rate and inverse inflation rates, (τdisc, ̃πdisc)
36:1571:97488:16:17:72:540:394:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:are determined under discretion, as in Proposition 4.  In this case, the optimal monetary policy is to rely
36:1572:97595:17:17:72:540:377:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:on the inflation tax:   ̃πdisc=   ̃π.  The base for this tax, i.e.  the money holdings of the old agents, will be
36:1573:97708:17:17:72:394:360:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:determined by the inflationary expectations they held in the prior period.
36:1574:97782:17:30:86:539:343:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:The incentive for maintaining policy’wit’is characterized by the following difference in agents’ welfare:
36:1575:97887:30:7:114:380:313:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f16:∆(A,i,m−1,p) = [Wwit(A,i,m−1)−Wdisc(A,i,m−1)] +β
36:1576:97935:7:0:366:389:306:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f16:1−β
36:1577:97938:0:33:390:540:313:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:[Vwit( ̃π∗)−Vdlg( ̃π∗,p)].(72)
36:1578:97968:33:16:86:540:280:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:HereWwit(A,i,m−1)−Wdisc(A,i,m−1)  is  the  immediate  gain  to  old  agents  from  deviating  to  full
36:1579:98070:16:17:71:540:264:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:discretion  from’wit’.   This  is  clearly  a  gain  since  the  non-distortionary  inflation  tax  is  desirableex  post,
36:1580:98192:17:17:72:330:247:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:particularly when agents are holding large money balances.
36:1581:98250:17:0:86:301:230:10:g_d0_f9:7:g_d0_f17:The punishment arises from the second term,β1−β
36:1582:98297:0:11:302:307:241:10:g_d0_f20:10:g_d0_f20:[
36:1583:98298:11:0:307:403:230:10:g_d0_f16:10:g_d0_f9:Vwit( ̃π∗)−Vdlg( ̃π∗,p)
36:1584:98321:0:11:403:408:241:10:g_d0_f20:10:g_d0_f20:]
36:1585:98322:11:16:408:540:230:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:, whereβ∈(0,1] is the rate at
36:1586:98351:16:17:71:540:214:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:which the monetary authority discounts successive generations.42Here the punishment for deviating from
36:1587:98453:17:15:71:539:197:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:policy’wit’is the continuing operation of the monetary authority under the strict inflation target regime.
36:1588:98559:15:12:79:539:182:6:g_d0_f15:8:g_d0_f14:40For the clarity of the exposition in this section, we assume that   ̃πis low enough so that the feasibility of’law’is not an
36:1589:98685:12:11:71:540:170:8:g_d0_f14:8:g_d0_f14:issue, i.e.   ̃πpAl> ̃π.  Further, we assume thatbis high enough, i.e.b > νm ̃π∗.  None of the results depend crucially on these
36:1590:98813:11:7:72:106:159:8:g_d0_f14:8:g_d0_f14:elements.
36:1591:98822:7:9:79:362:152:6:g_d0_f15:8:g_d0_f14:41Again, the market shutdown case is of no interest for the present analysis.
36:1592:98899:9:12:79:540:143:6:g_d0_f15:8:g_d0_f14:42This welfare criterion is not inconsistent with the one derived for the repayment vs.  default decision on debt.  As discussed
36:1593:99027:12:0:72:387:131:8:g_d0_f14:8:g_d0_f14:in 2.2, this decision has welfare consequences that are contained within a generation.
37:1594:99115:0:17:72:539:759:10:g_d0_f9:7:g_d0_f12:The idea here is that, like the ECB, the policy’wit’is built upon a basic commitment to an inflation target.43
37:1595:99225:17:17:71:539:742:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:As constructed, that inflation target is met on average by the policy and along the equilibrium path.  If policy
37:1596:99337:17:17:71:539:725:10:g_d0_f10:10:g_d0_f9:’wit’is not maintained, then the experiment with that form of intervention is over and the monetary authority
37:1597:99446:17:16:71:539:708:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:returns to its essential goal of strict inflation target.  In fact, resorting to the inflation target is a punishment
37:1598:99563:16:17:71:540:692:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:precisely because of the possibility of self-fulfilling debt crisis.  Indeed, sinceVwit( ̃π∗) =Vdlg( ̃π∗,1), we have
37:1599:99679:17:17:71:215:675:10:g_d0_f16:10:g_d0_f9:Vwit( ̃π∗)> Vdlg( ̃π∗,p) forp <1.
37:1600:99712:17:17:86:540:658:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:We evaluate the credibility of the policy’wit’whenever the capacity of the institution to anchor inflation
37:1601:99818:17:16:72:540:641:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:expectations is not challenged.  Accordingly, along the deviations considered,m−1=  ̃π∗.  If ∆(A,i, ̃π∗,p)≥0,
37:1602:99927:16:17:72:540:625:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:then policy’wit’is incentive compatible in state (A,i,p).  Using this construction, the’wit’policy can be
37:1603:100032:17:17:71:539:608:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:supported  in  an  equilibrium  without  commitment  if  the  costs  of  deviating  from  it  are  sufficiently  high.
37:1604:100150:17:24:71:112:591:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:Formally,
37:1605:100159:24:17:71:540:567:10:g_d0_f8:10:g_d0_f10:Proposition 6.If  the  probability  of  pessimism  is  sufficiently  high  andβclose  enough  to  unity,  then  the
37:1606:100274:17:17:71:539:550:10:g_d0_f10:10:g_d0_f10:monetary  authority  will  pursue  the  ’wit’  policy  in  all  states,  i.e.∆(A,i, ̃π∗,p)≥0for  allAandi∈[i,iδ].
37:1607:100387:17:24:72:191:533:10:g_d0_f10:10:g_d0_f10:Debt fragility is eliminated.
37:1608:100416:24:17:72:539:509:10:g_d0_f10:10:g_d0_f9:Proof.ClearlyWwit(A,i, ̃π∗)−Wdisc(A,i, ̃π∗)≤0 since the monetary authority operating under discretion
37:1609:100517:17:16:72:539:492:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:could replicate policy’wit’.  In fact from Proposition 4, it will choose   ̃π=  ̃π.  This inflation rate is higher
37:1610:100631:16:17:72:539:476:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:than that under policy’wit’for any (A,i).  Higher inflation relaxes the debt burden left to be serviced with
37:1611:100739:17:17:71:539:459:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:distortionary  taxation  and  unambiguously  increases  welfare.   Also  note  that  by  construction’wit’deters
37:1612:100851:17:16:71:397:442:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:state-contingent default.  A fortiori, no default is possible under discretion.
37:1613:100930:16:17:86:540:426:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f3:AsVdlg( ̃π∗,p)  is  increasing  inp,  ∆(A,i, ̃π∗,p)  is  decreasing  inp.   So  for  low  enoughp,Vwit( ̃π∗)−
37:1614:101039:17:17:71:540:409:10:g_d0_f16:10:g_d0_f9:Vdlg( ̃π∗,p) can be large.  Further, forβclose to unity,β1−β[Vwit( ̃π∗)−Vdlg( ̃π∗,p)] can be arbitrarily large.
37:1615:101150:17:25:71:445:392:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:Hence forpsufficiently small andβclose enough to unity, ∆(A,i, ̃π∗,p)>0 for allA.
37:1616:101231:25:16:86:539:367:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:This  proposition  nests  two  types  of  deviations  from  the  equilibrium  path.   First,  suppose  investors  in
37:1617:101347:16:17:72:539:351:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:periodt−1  believe  in  policy’wit’,  charge  the  fundamental  interest  rateiand  expect  the  unconditional
37:1618:101457:17:17:72:539:334:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:inflation target  ̃π∗in all states.  Still in periodtthe monetary authority operating under’wit’can choose to
37:1619:101566:17:16:72:540:317:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:deviate and resort to discretion.  The gain from this is the use of the non-distortionary inflation tax, which
37:1620:101676:16:17:72:539:301:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:is the highest forA=Al.  The cost is that’whatever it takes’is no longer credible.  But the foundation of
37:1621:101781:17:17:72:539:284:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:the monetary authority as following strict inflation targeting, i.e.delegation, is not altered.  If the conditions
37:1622:101895:17:17:72:503:267:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:of Proposition 6 are satisfied, the monetary authority does not deviate along the equilibrium path.
37:1623:101994:17:16:86:539:250:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:Providing incentives for the monetary authority along the equilibrium path is necessary but not sufficient
37:1624:102100:16:17:72:540:234:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:for’whatever  it  takes’to be incentive compatible.  Consider a deviation by investors in which they believe
37:1625:102208:17:17:72:540:217:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:there is a positive probability of default implyingi > i.  We maintain the integrity of the monetary authority
37:1626:102318:17:17:71:540:200:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:and  thus  anchor  inflationary  expectations  at   ̃π∗.44In  this  case,’wit’prescribes  to  implement{ ̃πpA}as
37:1627:102430:17:16:71:539:183:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:described in Lemma 6.  In this case, the incentive compatibility constraint will be binding in all states if it
37:1628:102541:16:15:71:540:167:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:binds whenA=Ah.  Indeed, to deliver the inflation targeton average, the central bank tightens monetary
37:1629:102643:15:12:79:540:152:6:g_d0_f15:8:g_d0_f14:43The deviation from’wit’to’disc’could be replaced by a deviation to the inflation target.  This would generate a smaller
37:1630:102764:12:7:72:256:140:8:g_d0_f14:8:g_d0_f14:short term gain, making it easier to support’wit’.
37:1631:102814:7:12:79:539:133:6:g_d0_f15:8:g_d0_f14:44As discussed earlier, policy’wit’applies only for interest rates below a level denotediδ.  For pessimism sufficiently high so
37:1632:102941:12:0:72:477:121:8:g_d0_f14:8:g_d0_f14:thati > iδ,’wit’prescribes default with probability one.  In that situation, there is no credibility to evaluate.
38:1633:103056:0:17:72:540:759:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:policy  whenever  the  realization  of  technology  is  high.   Still,  if  the  conditions  for  Proposition  6  hold,  the
38:1634:103180:17:17:72:539:742:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:monetary authority will have an incentive to intervene to preserve its reputation and follow policy ’wit’.  In
38:1635:103290:17:17:72:457:725:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:this case, the pessimism of the investors is not warranted, whatever the realization ofA.
38:1636:103379:17:16:86:540:708:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:The conditions for supporting policy’wit’have two components.  This first is the usual condition that
38:1637:103480:16:17:72:540:692:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:the monetary authority does not discount the future too heavily.  The second is not standard and involves
38:1638:103585:17:17:72:540:675:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:the strategic uncertainty of the model.  A gain from policy’wit’is the elimination of debt crisis that do arise
38:1639:103696:17:17:71:540:658:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:with probability (1−p) under the strict inflation target regime.  As this probability of pessimism gets larger,
38:1640:103807:17:16:71:539:641:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:the penalty associated with sticking to the inflation target regime is larger.  Accordingly, the higher the risk
38:1641:103919:16:17:71:539:625:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:of coordination failure under inflation targeting, the more credible it is for the central bank to promise to
38:1642:104028:17:17:71:330:608:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:undertake’whatever it takes’to counter pessimistic beliefs.
38:1643:104087:17:17:86:539:591:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:Finally, note that here we are not considering a deviation in which investors no longer trust the monetary
38:1644:104193:17:16:71:539:574:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:authority  to  meet  the  inflation  target  on  average.   Otherwise,  investors  may  hold  arbitrary  expectations
38:1645:104310:16:17:71:540:558:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:about future inflation, which would influence the gain from discretion relative to’wit’.  As argued in Section
38:1646:104420:17:17:71:539:541:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:4.2, the foundation for the credibility of the strict inflation target regime could be supported with the threat
38:1647:104532:17:40:71:220:524:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:of demonetization of the economy.
38:1648:104565:40:26:71:179:484:14:g_d0_f11:14:g_d0_f11:6    Conclusions
38:1649:104581:26:17:71:539:458:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:The goal of this paper was to determine whether monetary policy enhances or mitigates fiscal fragility.  Cast
38:1650:104690:17:17:71:539:441:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:as a real economy, the basic environment has fragile debt:  there are multiple valuations of government debt
38:1651:104798:17:17:71:233:424:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:depending on the beliefs of investors.
38:1652:104836:17:16:86:539:407:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:The effects of introducing monetary interventions depends on the commitment of the central bank.  If the
38:1653:104940:16:17:71:539:391:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:central bank is committed to an inflation target, then debt fragility remains.  If the central bank is allowed
38:1654:105050:17:17:71:539:374:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:full discretion, then the presence of an inelastic source of finance through seignorage is internalized by private
38:1655:105164:17:17:71:495:357:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:agents.  Any temptation to inflate the real value of debt is anticipated and debt fragility remains.
38:1656:105264:17:16:86:539:340:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:Finally, we analyze how a committed central bank can deter debt fragility, by designing a specific monetary
38:1657:105371:16:17:71:539:324:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:policy rule.  We devise a state contingent intervention that eliminates pessimistic evaluations of government
38:1658:105480:17:17:71:539:307:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:debt.  The policy requires the monetary authority to implement a countercyclical policy, that erodes the real
38:1659:105589:17:17:71:539:290:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:value of debt and provides resources, through seignorage, in times of low productivity and thus low revenue.
38:1660:105697:17:16:71:539:273:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:By supporting the fiscal authorities in these states, the incentive for default is eliminated.  Sovereign debt is
38:1661:105810:16:17:71:539:257:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:no longer subject to multiple valuations driven by investors’ sentiments.  Interestingly, the credibility of this
38:1662:105923:17:17:71:378:240:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:monetary strategy increases with the risk of a self-fulfilling debt crisis.
38:1663:105998:17:17:86:539:223:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:A number of extensions are worth consideration.  First, the paper studies the extremes of commitment
38:1664:106098:17:16:71:540:206:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f16:and discretion.  An interesting middle case would be stochastic commitment.  A government acting in periodt
38:1665:106205:16:17:71:540:190:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:would be allowed to adjust its policy in periodt+1 with a probability less than one.  This partial commitment
38:1666:106314:17:17:71:356:173:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:would create a cost of high inflation and thus enrich the analysis.
38:1667:106381:17:16:86:539:156:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:Second, the model is dynamic but the fiscal policy is within a generation.  Thus we have assumed away
38:1668:106482:16:17:71:404:140:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:the possibilities of debt turnover and intertemporal punishments for default.
38:1669:106559:17:0:86:539:123:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:Third, our analysis has underlined that the capacity of the central bank to stabilize debt valuations rely
39:1670:106667:0:17:72:540:759:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:on the issuance of non contingent nominal assets labelled in domestic currency.  It does not apply to real,
39:1671:106774:17:17:72:522:742:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:indexed debt or debt issued in foreign currency.  Allowing governments this choice would be of interest.
39:1672:106878:17:17:86:539:725:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:Finally,  as  in  many  other  studies,  the  outcome  with  discretion  imposes  an  upper  bound  on  inflation.
39:1673:106992:17:16:72:540:708:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:Providing further micro foundations for this bound remains an open area.  Perhaps a political economy model
39:1674:107099:16:41:72:527:692:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:that stresses the redistribution aspects of labor income vs inflation tax would be a productive approach.
39:1675:107204:41:29:72:165:651:14:g_d0_f11:14:g_d0_f11:7    Appendix
39:1676:107217:29:23:72:370:622:12:g_d0_f11:12:g_d0_f11:7.1    Welfare under Repayment and under Default
39:1677:107265:23:17:72:540:599:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:As explained in section (2.2), the repayment vs.  default decision in this environment is a discrete choice that
39:1678:107377:17:32:72:475:582:10:g_d0_f9:10:g_d0_f9:affects only the welfare of old agents.  Hence, the welfare criteria of interest forD∈{r,d}is:

39:1686:107514:0:11:379:384:561:10:g_d0_f20:10:g_d0_f20:[
39:1687:107515:11:0:384:428:550:10:g_d0_f16:10:g_d0_f16:cIo(D)−n
